     <header class="section__header">

     <!-- end of section__header -->
     <div class="loc section-content section__content ">
      <ul class="comp masonry-list mntl-masonry-list mntl-block l-container" data-tracking-container="true" id="masonry-list_3-0">
       <li class="comp masonry-list__item mntl-block" id="masonry-list__item_5-0">
        <a class="comp card" href="https://www.thespruce.com/feng-shui-101-4118350" id="card_5-0">
         <div class="loc card__header">
          <div class="comp card__media image" id="card__media_5-0">
